*Yuze Chen,Yuan Zhou,Baichuan Mo,Jie Ying,Yufei Ruan,Zhou Ye*

Main category: math.OC

Relevance: 15.0

TL;DR: 该论文研究具有随机补给过程的在线线性规划问题，针对三种分布类型设计了不同算法，获得了从√T到log²T的遗憾界，并建立了理论下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统在线线性规划假设初始库存已知且固定，但实际运营场景（如电商履约、易腐供应链、可再生能源系统）中资源是逐渐累积的，初始库存可能很小甚至为零。这种随机补给过程改变了问题的结构，带来了持续的缺货风险，需要新的算法和理论分析。

Method: 针对三种分布类型分别设计算法：1）有界分布：设计算法获得√T遗憾；2）有限支撑分布：对非退化LP实例获得log T遗憾，对退化实例建立√T下界；3）连续支撑非退化分布：设计两阶段"先积累后转换"算法获得log²T遗憾。

Result: 在有界分布下获得√T遗憾；在有限支撑非退化分布下获得log T遗憾，退化实例有√T下界；在连续支撑非退化分布下获得log²T遗憾。这些结果几乎完全刻画了补给型OLP的最优遗憾界。

Conclusion: 随机补给过程显著改变了在线线性规划问题的性质，需要专门设计的算法。论文针对不同分布类型提供了近乎最优的算法，并通过实证验证了这些算法优于传统OLP方法的适应性版本。

Abstract: We study an online linear programming (OLP) model in which inventory is not provided upfront but instead arrives gradually through an exogenous stochastic replenishment process. This replenishment-based formulation captures operational settings, such as e-commerce fulfillment, perishable supply chains, and renewable-powered systems, where resources are accumulated gradually and initial inventories are small or zero. The introduction of dispersed, uncertain replenishment fundamentally alters the structure of classical OLPs, creating persistent stockout risk and eliminating advance knowledge of the total budget.
  We develop new algorithms and regret analyses for three major distributional regimes studied in the OLP literature: bounded distributions, finite-support distributions, and continuous-support distributions with a non-degeneracy condition. For bounded distributions, we design an algorithm that achieves $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(\sqrt{T})$ regret. For finite-support distributions with a non-degenerate induced LP, we obtain $\mathcal{O}(\log T)$ regret, and we establish an $Ω(\sqrt{T})$ lower bound for degenerate instances, demonstrating a sharp separation from the classical setting where $\mathcal{O}(1)$ regret is achievable. For continuous-support, non-degenerate distributions, we develop a two-stage accumulate-then-convert algorithm that achieves $\mathcal{O}(\log^2 T)$ regret, comparable to the $\mathcal{O}(\log T)$ regret in classical OLPs. Together, these results provide a near-complete characterization of the optimal regret achievable in OLP with replenishment. Finally, we empirically evaluate our algorithms and demonstrate their advantages over natural adaptations of classical OLP methods in the replenishment setting.

</details>


### [319] [Semi-Supervised Mixture Models under the Concept of Missing at Radom with Margin Confidence and Aranda Ordaz Function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.14631)
*Jinyang Liao,Ziyang Lyu*

Main category: stat.ML

Relevance: 15.0

TL;DR: 提出了一种用于高斯混合模型（GMM）的半监督学习框架，专门处理随机缺失（MAR）机制。该方法通过建模分类不确定性来参数化缺失机制，使用Aranda Ordaz链接函数捕捉不确定性与缺失概率之间的非对称关系，并开发了高效的ECM算法进行联合参数估计和缺失标签补全。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现实世界的半监督学习场景中，标签经常以随机缺失（MAR）的方式出现，即缺失概率取决于观察到的数据。传统的半监督学习方法通常忽略缺失机制，这可能导致估计偏差。本文旨在开发一个能够显式建模缺失机制的框架，以提高分类性能的可靠性。

Method: 1. 将缺失概率参数化为分类不确定性的函数；2. 引入边界置信度来量化分类不确定性；3. 使用Aranda Ordaz（AO）链接函数灵活捕捉不确定性与缺失概率之间的非对称关系；4. 开发期望条件最大化（ECM）算法，联合估计GMM和缺失机制的所有参数；5. 基于拟合的混合模型，使用贝叶斯分类器补全缺失标签。

Result: 该方法有效减轻了忽略缺失机制引起的偏差，增强了半监督学习的鲁棒性。在具有大量缺失标签的现实MAR场景中，这种不确定性感知框架能够提供可靠的分类性能。

Conclusion: 本文提出的半监督学习框架通过显式建模缺失机制，成功解决了MAR场景下的标签缺失问题。该方法结合了不确定性量化和灵活的链接函数，为高斯混合模型在半监督学习中的应用提供了更可靠和鲁棒的解决方案。

Abstract: This paper presents a semi-supervised learning framework for Gaussian mixture modelling under a Missing at Random (MAR) mechanism. The method explicitly parameterizes the missingness mechanism by modelling the probability of missingness as a function of classification uncertainty. To quantify classification uncertainty, we introduce margin confidence and incorporate the Aranda Ordaz (AO) link function to flexibly capture the asymmetric relationships between uncertainty and missing probability. Based on this formulation, we develop an efficient Expectation Conditional Maximization (ECM) algorithm that jointly estimates all parameters appearing in both the Gaussian mixture model (GMM) and the missingness mechanism, and subsequently imputes the missing labels by a Bayesian classifier derived from the fitted mixture model. This method effectively alleviates the bias induced by ignoring the missingness mechanism while enhancing the robustness of semi-supervised learning. The resulting uncertainty-aware framework delivers reliable classification performance in realistic MAR scenarios with substantial proportions of missing labels.

</details>


### [320] [RANDSMAPs: Random-Feature/multi-Scale Neural Decoders with Mass Preservation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.14794)
*Dimitrios G. Patsatzis,Alessandro Della Pia,Lucia Russo,Constantinos Siettos*

Main category: math.NA

Relevance: 15.0

TL;DR: RANDSMAPs是一种基于数值分析的、可解释的神经解码器，专门设计用于在流形学习中解决具有挑战性的不适定原像问题时显式地遵守守恒定律。该方法通过随机傅里叶特征神经网络与径向基函数插值的等价性证明，建立了理论基础，并引入多尺度变体来捕捉多尺度结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在流形学习中，原像问题是一个具有挑战性的不适定问题。现有方法通常无法显式地遵守物理系统中的守恒定律（如质量守恒）。本文旨在开发一种数值分析启发的、可解释的神经解码器，能够明确地尊重守恒定律，同时保持计算效率。

Method: 1. 证明了vanilla随机傅里叶特征神经网络与径向基函数插值以及双扩散映射解码器在确定性极限下的等价性
2. 建立了RANDSMAP的理论基础，并引入其多尺度变体以捕捉多尺度结构
3. 制定并推导了相应约束优化问题的闭式解，证明了质量保持特性
4. 在三个基准问题/数据集上评估性能：具有冲击波的Lighthill-Whitham-Richards交通流PDE、2D旋转MRI脑图像和Hughes人群动力学PDE

Result: RANDSMAPs在低计算成本下实现了高重建精度，并在单机精度下保持了质量守恒。即使在vanilla公式中，该方案仍然适用于经典的原像问题（即不施加质量保持约束的情况）。

Conclusion: RANDSMAPs提供了一种数值分析启发的、可解释的神经解码器框架，能够显式地尊重守恒定律，在流形学习的原像问题上表现出色，同时保持计算效率。该方法在需要物理约束保持的应用中具有重要价值。

Abstract: We introduce RANDSMAPs (Random-feature/multi-scale neural decoders with Mass Preservation), numerical analysis-informed, explainable neural decoders designed to explicitly respect conservation laws when solving the challenging ill-posed pre-image problem in manifold learning. We start by proving the equivalence of vanilla random Fourier feature neural networks to Radial Basis Function interpolation and the double Diffusion Maps (based on Geometric Harmonics) decoders in the deterministic limit. We then establish the theoretical foundations for RANDSMAP and introduce its multiscale variant to capture structures across multiple scales. We formulate and derive the closed-form solution of the corresponding constrained optimization problem and prove the mass preservation property. Numerically, we assess the performance of RANDSMAP on three benchmark problems/datasets with mass preservation obtained by the Lighthill-Whitham-Richards traffic flow PDE with shock waves, 2D rotated MRI brain images, and the Hughes crowd dynamics PDEs. We demonstrate that RANDSMAPs yield high reconstruction accuracy at low computational cost and maintain mass conservation at single-machine precision. In its vanilla formulation, the scheme remains applicable to the classical pre-image problem, i.e., when mass-preservation constraints are not imposed.

</details>


### [321] [ExoMiner++ 2.0: Vetting TESS Full-Frame Image Transit Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.14877)
*Miguel J. S. Martinho,Hamed Valizadegan,Jon M. Jenkins,Douglas A. Caldwell,Joseph D. Twicken,Ben Tofflemire,Marziye Jafariyazani*

Main category: astro-ph.EP

Relevance: 15.0

TL;DR: 将ExoMiner++ 2.0模型从TESS 2分钟数据扩展到全帧图像(FFI)光变曲线，用于大规模行星与非行星分类，支持未来系外行星群体研究和后续观测优先级排序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: TESS全帧图像(FFI)为数百万恒星提供光度时间序列，但FFI数据在凌星识别和验证方面存在额外挑战。需要将现有的ExoMiner++框架扩展到FFI领域，以利用完整的TESS数据集进行系外行星发现。

Method: 应用ExoMiner++ 2.0（最初为TESS 2分钟数据开发）到FFI光变曲线，构建统一的验证目录，评估不同观测条件下的模型性能，进行大规模行星与非行星分类。

Result: ExoMiner++ 2.0在FFI领域表现出良好的泛化能力，尽管长周期数据存在固有局限性，但仍能有效区分行星信号、天体物理假阳性信号和仪器伪影。

Conclusion: 该工作成功将ExoMiner++扩展到完整的TESS数据集，为未来系外行星群体研究和后续观测优先级排序提供了有力工具。

Abstract: The Transiting Exoplanet Survey Satellite (TESS) Full-Frame Images (FFIs) provide photometric time series for millions of stars, enabling transit searches beyond the limited set of pre-selected 2-minute targets. However, FFIs present additional challenges for transit identification and vetting. In this work, we apply ExoMiner++ 2.0, an adaptation of the ExoMiner++ framework originally developed for TESS 2-minute data, to FFI light curves. The model is used to perform large-scale planet versus non-planet classification of Threshold Crossing Events across the sectors analyzed in this study. We construct a uniform vetting catalog of all evaluated signals and assess model performance under different observing conditions. We find that ExoMiner++ 2.0 generalizes effectively to the FFI domain, providing robust discrimination between planetary signals, astrophysical false positives, and instrumental artifacts despite the limitations inherent to longer cadence data. This work extends the applicability of ExoMiner++ to the full TESS dataset and supports future population studies and follow-up prioritization.

</details>


### [322] [One scale to rule them all: interpretable multi-scale Deep Learning for predicting cell survival after proton and carbon ion irradiation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.15106)
*Giulio Bordieri,Giorgio Cartechini,Anna Bianchi,Anna Selva,Valeria Conte,Marta Missiaggia,Francesco G. Cordoni*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

Relevance: 15.0

TL;DR: 开发了一个可解释的深度学习模型，用于预测质子和碳离子辐照后的细胞存活率，结合了纳米剂量学和微剂量学等多尺度特征，在保持高预测准确性的同时提供决策透明度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 辐射场的物理特性与生物损伤之间的关系是放射治疗和辐射防护的核心问题，但能量沉积的空间尺度与生物效应之间的联系尚未完全理解。需要开发能够解释不同能量沉积尺度贡献的预测模型。

Method: 开发了可解释的深度学习模型，使用顺序注意力机制突出相关特征。模型结合了LET（线性能量转移）、纳米剂量学和微剂量学量（通过MC-Startrack和Open-TOPAS模拟），实现多尺度表征。在PIDE数据集上进行训练和测试。

Result: 模型在预测体外实验的相对生物效应（RBE）方面表现出高准确性。多尺度特征被同时利用，没有单一空间尺度占主导地位。较小空间域定义的量通常具有更大影响，而LET的作用较小。

Conclusion: 开发的可解释深度学习模型成功预测了质子和碳离子辐照后的细胞存活率，提供了对多尺度能量沉积贡献的洞察，强调了较小空间尺度特征的重要性，为放射生物学研究提供了新的分析工具。

Abstract: The relationship between the physical characteristics of the radiation field and biological damage is central to both radiotherapy and radioprotection, yet the link between spatial scales of energy deposition and biological effects remains not entirely understood. To address this, we developed an interpretable deep learning model that predicts cell survival after proton and carbon ion irradiation, leveraging sequential attention to highlight relevant features and provide insight into the contribution of different energy deposition scales. Trained and tested on the PIDE dataset, our model incorporates, beside LET, nanodosimetric and microdosimetric quantities simulated with MC-Startrack and Open-TOPAS, enabling multi-scale characterization. While achieving high predictive accuracy, our approach also emphasizes transparency in decision-making. We demonstrate high accuracy in predicting RBE for in vitro experiments. Multiple scales are utilized concurrently, with no single spatial scale being predominant. Quantities defined at smaller spatial domains generally have a greater influence, whereas the LET plays a lesser role.

</details>


### [323] [From Observation to Prediction: LSTM for Vehicle Lane Change Forecasting on Highway On/Off-Ramps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.14848)
*Mohamed Abouras,Catherine M. Elias*

Main category: cs.LG

Relevance: 5.0

TL;DR: 该论文研究高速公路匝道区域的车辆行为预测，使用多层LSTM架构在ExiD无人机数据集上进行训练，比较了匝道区域与直线高速路段的预测性能差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高速公路匝道区域是研究不足的路段，这些区域引入了更高的交通交互变化性。预测车辆在这些区域的行为可以减少不确定性影响并提高道路安全性。

Method: 使用多层LSTM架构在ExiD无人机数据集上训练匝道区域模型，测试了不同的预测时间范围和模型工作流程，比较了匝道区域与直线高速路段的差异。

Result: 结果显示在最多4秒的时间范围内表现出良好前景：匝道区域最大时间范围的预测准确率约为76%，而一般高速公路场景为94%。

Conclusion: 匝道区域的车辆行为预测具有挑战性但可行，多层LSTM架构在4秒时间范围内能提供有效的预测，为高速公路安全应用提供了基础。

Abstract: On and off-ramps are understudied road sections even though they introduce a higher level of variation in highway interactions. Predicting vehicles' behavior in these areas can decrease the impact of uncertainty and increase road safety. In this paper, the difference between this Area of Interest (AoI) and a straight highway section is studied. Multi-layered LSTM architecture to train the AoI model with ExiD drone dataset is utilized. In the process, different prediction horizons and different models' workflow are tested. The results show great promise on horizons up to 4 seconds with prediction accuracy starting from about 76% for the AoI and 94% for the general highway scenarios on the maximum horizon.

</details>
